in need,’ but really, it’s cool to have just any kind of friend. Making new friends, though, is not easy. Maybe you’re on the lookout for the Samwise to your Frodo, so you can develop a friendship so legendary it spawns the filthiest kind of fan fiction. Or maybe you just want someone with whom to shoot the shit with every once in awhile. Whatever your goals may be, Me3 hopes to be the catalyst that ensures platonic Cupid aims his arrows the right way. The newly launched app available on Android and iOS promises to find you like-minded people who are fun to hang out with, and possibly spawn a long lasting friendship. It does so by putting you into same-sex groups of three. The Pico Model C by PicoBrew is a smart appliance that enables anyone to brew five liters of craft beer using ingredient-and-recipe packets (PicoPaks) from craft breweries across the globe. &nbsp; &nbsp; To use the device, users insert their PicoPak into Pico and add water. They then personalize their beer; brew it for approximately two hours; ferment the brew in a beer keg; transfer and carbonate; and enjoy. As with many smart devices today, there’s a companion marketplace for PicoPaks known as the BrewMarketplace. It enables customers to find craft beer by exploring user reviews, and through communicating directly with the brewers themselves. Additionally, it allows users to discover recipes, support the local craft brew community, and explore a variety of beers from anywhere. Guttenberg\" class=\"avatar avatar-96 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-96 alignnone photo\">          </div>\n                          <span class=\"sm-post-meta\">BY Daniel A. Guttenberg</span>\n              </div>\n    </div>\n          <div class=\"sm-entry-content\">\n        <a class=\"sm-excerpt-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/ive-got-ui-under-my-skin/\">\n          <p>If you think employee drug tests are invasive, you definitely don’t want to work at Epicenter. This Swedish co-working space/startup facilitator has been digging a little deeper, implanting RFID chips into its workers and members to track their every move. &nbsp; OK, so the program is completely voluntary and has way more to do with convenience than security. Implantees can do things like open doors and charge things to expense accounts with a wave of their radio-wave-transmitting hand. The company doesn’t actually monitor them (as far as we know) but as one of the first larger-scale implementers of implant technology, Epicenter has been garnering all kinds of headlines. The Hype The cool factor of implantables is obvious…one might say it sits right on the surface. Something as simple and innocuous as a RFID chip can, with appropriate receivers in the environment, be used to do almost anything. Users and developers are convinced that we are reaching a point where this will redefine manufacturing in a way major companies cannot yet conceive. Despite that analysis, it seems that there is one company striving to meet the modern idea. Boeing has recently announced that it will start using 3D printed parts on their airplanes to cut costs. For those not familiar with the name Boeing is a major aerospace company. They’re known for the production of airplanes, rockets, and satellites on a worldwide scale. This week they announced that their newest airliner the 787 Dreamliner would use 3D printed parts made from structural titanium. Not only is the amplifier extremely portable, but it also links to any smartphone to make mixing in effects and backing tracks a breeze.      SnapMunk WTF: DDoS Attack, VR Harassment , Smartwatch Fizzle, AirPod Delay            </a>\n          </h2>\n                            </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n\n    \t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t wrap-->\n\t      <div class=\"sm-row-heading\">\n\t        <h2 class=\"sm-col-12\">TRENDING</h2>\n\t      </div>\n\t      <div class=\"sm-row\"><!--start excerpt post row-->\n\t    \t        <div class=\"sm-front-excerpt-post\"><!--start excerpt post-->\n    <a href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/ai-powered-mirror-computer/\">\n      <img width=\"375\" height=\"150\" src=\"https://d2ymzkn1ailq93.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/11101616/duo-mirror-sm-featured-375x150.jpg\" class=\"sm-thumb wp-post-image\" alt=\"duo mirror sm featured\">    </a>\n    <div class=\"sm-entry-header\">\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic\">\n                                      <span class=\"sm-post-tag sm-tag-link\">STARTUPS</span>\n                        </div>\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic sm-light\">\n        <h2 class=\"sm-entry-title\">\n          <a class=\"sm-post-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/ai-powered-mirror-computer/\">\n            Duo, An AI-Powered, Voice-Commanded Mirror-Computer          </a>\n        </h2>\n      </div>\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic sm-light\">\n                          <div class=\"sm-author-avatar\">\n            <img src=\"https://d2ymzkn1ailq93.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/17231044/prateek-jose-sm-avatar.png\" width=\"50\" height=\"50\" alt=\"Prateek Jose\" class=\"avatar avatar-96 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-96 alignnone photo\">          </div>\n                          <span class=\"sm-post-meta\">BY Prateek Jose</span>\n              </div>\n    </div>\n          <div class=\"sm-entry-content\">\n        <a class=\"sm-excerpt-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/ai-powered-mirror-computer/\">\n          <p>A while back, Mark Zuckerberg showed off Jarvis, an AI personal assistant he had built to help around the home–his home. Unfortunately, the technology has yet to go into production. For those of us hoping for something similar, there’s Duo, an AI-powered computer with a mirror-based interface that’s meant to serve as mission control for your soon-to-be smart home. It won’t shoot your clothes at you or speak in Mandarin like Jarvis (yet), but Duo has its very own bag o’ tricks. Duo looks like a mirror, but its creators insist it’s not a smart mirror; they’d much rather call it a computer that happens to have a reflective screen. The reason it does have a reflective screen is that the device is a pretty substantial 27 inches in height. Getting such a large piece of additional equipment to blend in with the interiors in a room would be a…</p>\n        </a>\n      </div>\n      </div><!--end excerpt post-->\n  \t    \t        <div class=\"sm-front-excerpt-post\"><!--start excerpt post-->\n    <a href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/pixie-tracker-item-finder-hide-go-seek-stuff/\">\n      <img width=\"375\" height=\"150\" src=\"https://d2ymzkn1ailq93.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/11101924/pixie-tracker-sm-featured-375x150.jpg\" class=\"sm-thumb wp-post-image\" alt=\"pixie tracker sm featured\">    </a>\n    <div class=\"sm-entry-header\">\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic\">\n                                      <span class=\"sm-post-tag sm-tag-link\">STARTUPS</span>\n                        </div>\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic sm-light\">\n        <h2 class=\"sm-entry-title\">\n          <a class=\"sm-post-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/pixie-tracker-item-finder-hide-go-seek-stuff/\">\n            The Pixie Tracker, An Item Finder To Stop Playing Hide-and-Go-Seek With Your Stuff          </a>\n        </h2>\n      </div>\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic sm-light\">\n                          <div class=\"sm-author-avatar\">\n            <img src=\"https://d2ymzkn1ailq93.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/08103059/Benda-headshot-300x250.jpg\" width=\"96\" height=\"80\" alt=\"Brenda Barron\" class=\"avatar avatar-96 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-96 alignnone photo\">          </div>\n                          <span class=\"sm-post-meta\">BY Brenda Barron</span>\n              </div>\n    </div>\n          <div class=\"sm-entry-content\">\n        <a class=\"sm-excerpt-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/pixie-tracker-item-finder-hide-go-seek-stuff/\">\n          <p>Our lives are hectic enough. Adding in extra stresses like new jobs, growing families, and more technological devices can spell disaster for organization. It’s easy to get sidetracked and lose touch with the essential tangible items we need to work, drive the kids to soccer practice, or pay the pizza delivery guy. According to a study by esure home insurance, it appears that losing items like keys, wallets, and other common items we use on a regular basis is more common than we think. The study found that three-quarters of all lost items are in the home. They also noted that adults lose, on average, ten minutes of every day searching for these items. Those are ten minutes people can’t afford to give up when they’re already running late for work, school, or meetups. So what’s the answer? In comes&nbsp;Pixie with a solution to a problem we all too commonly…</p>\n        </a>\n      </div>\n      </div><!--end excerpt post-->\n  \t    \t        <div class=\"sm-front-excerpt-post\"><!--start excerpt post-->\n    <a href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/australia-vs-apple-sued/\">\n      <img width=\"375\" height=\"150\" src=\"https://d2ymzkn1ailq93.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/11102343/australia-apple-sm-featured-375x150.jpg\" class=\"sm-thumb wp-post-image\" alt=\"australia apple sm featured\">    </a>\n    <div class=\"sm-entry-header\">\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic\">\n                                      <span class=\"sm-post-tag sm-tag-link\">INDUSTRY TRENDS</span>\n                        </div>\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic sm-light\">\n        <h2 class=\"sm-entry-title\">\n          <a class=\"sm-post-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/australia-vs-apple-sued/\">\n            Australia Vs. Apple; Yes Apple Is Being Sued By Australia          </a>\n        </h2>\n      </div>\n      <div class=\"sm-row-basic sm-light\">\n                          <div class=\"sm-author-avatar\">\n            <img src=\"https://d2ymzkn1ailq93.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2017/04/20183048/michael-chindamo-sm-avatar.jpg\" width=\"50\" height=\"50\" alt=\"Michael Chindamo\" class=\"avatar avatar-96 wp-user-avatar wp-user-avatar-96 alignnone photo\">          </div>\n                          <span class=\"sm-post-meta\">BY Michael Chindamo</span>\n              </div>\n    </div>\n          <div class=\"sm-entry-content\">\n        <a class=\"sm-excerpt-link\" href=\"https://www.snapmunk.com/australia-vs-apple-sued/\">\n          <p>It seems corporate shenanigans are becoming an international incident. We spoke on this issue previously along with Apple’s other recent failings but that that wasn’t the end of it. As it is Apple is facing a difficult challenge in Australia where the laws protecting consumers are not so favorable to companies when it comes to third party repairs. As many of you know Apple has a policy that if someone were to take their iPhone to a third party repair place, they can brick that phone. And they have. For those that don’t know, to brick a digital device is to make it completely inoperable. In short, it is little more than a brick of plastic. Hence the term.&nbsp; It’s an option more popularly used when one’s phone is stolen to prevent resale or loss of personal data. Apple was asked, by consumers, to restore their devices. The company&nbsp;refused, citing…</p>\n        </a>\n      </div>\n      </div><!--end excerpt post-->\n  \t    \t      </div><!--end excerpt post row-->\n\t    </div><!--end excerpt post wrap-->\n\t
